## Idea

Transpositions are permutations that swap two elements.

## Definitions

### Transpositions

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5414" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5421" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#5421" class="Module">_</a>

### Any transposition on a type equipped with a counting is a standard transposition

        <a id="23906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23907" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#6218" class="Function">has-decidable-equality-count</a> <a id="23936" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#12832" class="Bound">eX</a> <a id="23939" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23940" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="23944" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23945" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="23949" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#13263" class="Function">two-elements-transposition</a><a id="23975" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="23978" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23751" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23979" class="Symbol">)</a>

        <a id="24066" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24067" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#6218" class="Function">has-decidable-equality-count</a> <a id="24096" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#12832" class="Bound">eX</a> <a id="24099" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24100" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="24104" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24105" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="24109" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#13263" class="Function">two-elements-transposition</a><a id="24135" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24138" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23753" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24139" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Transpositions can be transported along equivalences

          <a id="29914" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29916" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="29926" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="29928" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24270" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="29930" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="29933" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8446" class="Function">transposition</a> <a id="29947" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29713" class="Bound">t</a><a id="29948" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29950" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="29953" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5721" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="29963" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24270" class="Bound">e</a><a id="29964" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="29977" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29979" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29154" class="Function">correct-transposition-conjugation-equiv-list</a> <a id="30024" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29715" class="Bound">li</a> <a id="30027" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29719" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30028" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="30031" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
          <a id="30043" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30045" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a>
            <a id="30060" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30062" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="30064" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30064" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="30066" class="Symbol">→</a>
              <a id="30082" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a>
                <a id="30108" class="Symbol">((((</a><a id="30112" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24270" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="30114" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30117" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8446" class="Function">transposition</a> <a id="30131" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29713" class="Bound">t</a><a id="30132" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30134" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30137" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30064" class="Bound">g</a><a id="30138" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30140" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30143" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#11007" class="Function">permutation-list-transpositions</a> <a id="30175" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29715" class="Bound">li</a><a id="30177" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30179" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30182" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5721" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="30192" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24270" class="Bound">e</a><a id="30193" class="Symbol">)</a>
                <a id="30211" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30213" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29719" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30214" class="Symbol">))</a>
            <a id="30229" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30231" href="foundation.equivalences.html#14415" class="Function">left-inverse-law-equiv</a> <a id="30254" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24270" class="Bound">e</a><a id="30255" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
### For all `n : ℕ`, for each transposition of `Fin n`, there exists a matching transposition in `Fin (succ-ℕ n)`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Fin-succ-Fin-transposition"></a><a id="30388" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30388" class="Function">Fin-succ-Fin-transposition</a> <a id="30415" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30418" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30418" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="30420" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30422" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1530" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="30423" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30425" class="Symbol">→</a> 
  <a id="30430" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30432" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a>

    <a id="30474" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30476" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="30478" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30478" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30480" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30482" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5208" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="30498" class="Number">2</a> <a id="30500" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30501" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="30503" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30504" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2393" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="30508" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30418" class="Bound">n</a><a id="30509" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30511" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="30514" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30514" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="30516" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30518" href="foundation-core.decidable-propositions.html#872" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="30538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30539" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30478" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30541" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30514" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30542" class="Symbol">)))))</a> <a id="30548" class="Symbol">→</a> 
    <a id="30555" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30557" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a>

      <a id="30612" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30614" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="30616" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30616" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30618" class="Symbol">→</a>
        <a id="30628" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5208" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="30644" class="Number">2</a>
          <a id="30656" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30658" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="30660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30661" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2393" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="30665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30666" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1564" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="30673" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30418" class="Bound">n</a><a id="30674" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="30677" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="30680" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30680" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="30682" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30684" href="foundation-core.decidable-propositions.html#872" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="30704" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30705" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30616" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30707" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30680" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30708" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
